							<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading">
								<span dir="auto">Law of Inertia League</span>
							</h1>

								<div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="mw-parser-output"><div class="ambox-wrapper"><div class="ambox wiki-bordercolor-dark wiki-backgroundcolor-light ambox-red"><table><tbody><tr><td class="ambox-image"><img alt="" src="/commons/images/4/4c/Emblem-important.svg" width="40" height="40" loading="lazy" /></td><td class="ambox-text">This tournament page was previously <b>moved to <a href="/dota2/Help:User_page" title="Help:User page">Userspace</a> because it did not meet Liquipedia's <a href="/dota2/Liquipedia:How_to_Contribute#Tournaments" title="Liquipedia:How to Contribute">standards for inclusion in the main article space</a></b> at the time. Liquipedia staff has deemed this tournament untrustworthy.</td></tr></tbody></table></div></div>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Format">Format</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/dota2/index.php?title=Law_of_Inertia_League/1&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Format">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>Two 6-team groups with <abbr title="Best-of-three">Bo3</abbr> round-robin
<ul><li>Top 2 teams of each group advance to the upper bracket of the Playoffs</li>
<li>3rd and 4th place of each group advance to lower bracket of the Playoffs</li>
<li>Other teams are eliminated</li></ul></li>
<li><abbr title="Best-of-three">Bo3</abbr> Double-elimination Playoffs, include a <abbr title="Best-of-five">Bo5</abbr> Grand Final.</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Prize_Pool">Prize Pool</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/dota2/index.php?title=Law_of_Inertia_League/1&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Prize Pool">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
